     var _wallpaperAdvertisementSettled = undefined;
 
     get_wallpaperAdvertisementSettled = function () {
         return _wallpaperAdvertisementSettled;
     };
 
     resolve_wallpaperAdvertisementSettled = function (value) {
         if (typeof value !== 'undefined' && typeof _wallpaperAdvertisementSettled === 'undefined') {
             _wallpaperAdvertisementSettled = value;

     var checkWallpaperAdvertisement = function () {

   <script type="text/javascript">
    //<![CDATA[
 
 // <!--
 // This code below extracts the contents of the
 // location.search and conveniently seperates
 // the name and value into a usable form.
 // Don't alter this code.
 //  -->
 function replace(str, from, to) {
     var i = str.indexOf(from);
     if (!from || !str || i == -1) return str;
     var newstr = str.substring(0, i) + to;
     if (i+from.length < str.length)
         newstr += replace(str.substring(
         i+from.length,str.length),from,to);
     return newstr;
 }
 function getQry(nm)
 {
     if (!location.search) return '';
     var i, j, qry;
     qry = location.search.substring(1);
     i = qry.indexOf(nm)+nm.length+1;
     if (i == nm.length) return '';
     j = qry.indexOf('&',i);
     if (j+1) qry = qry.substring(i,j);
     else     qry = qry.substring(i);
     return unescape(replace(qry, '+', ' '));
 }
 
 function substitute(str, from, to) {
     var i = str.indexOf(from);
     if (!from || !str || i == -1) return str;
     var newstr = str.substring(0, i);
     if (i+from.length < str.length)
         newstr += replace(str.substring(
         i+from.length,str.length),from);
     return newstr;
 
 }
 function convert(nm)
 {
     if (!location.search) return '';
     var i, j, qry;
     qry = location.search.substring(1);
     i = qry.indexOf(nm)+nm.length+1;
     if (i == nm.length) return '';
     j = qry.indexOf('&',i);
     if (j+1) qry = qry.substring(i,j);
     else     qry = qry.substring(i);
     return unescape(substitute(qry, '+'));
 }

 var newx;

   if (getQry('style') || cssval) {
     newVal=(cssval) ? cssval : getQry('style');
     newx = x + "?style=" +  newVal;
   }
   else {
     newx = x;
   }
      windowabandon = window.open(newx,y,'width=800,height=600,toolbar=0,location=0,directories=0,status=0,scrollbars=1,menubar=0,resizable=1');
 }
 function aolcsscheck(){
   var aolcss = new Array ('aolboxoffice','aolsvcboxoffice','aolsvcsportsbox','aolsvcmusicbox','africanaboxoffice','nsboxoffice');
   for(y=0;y < aolcss.length;y++){
       if(document.URL.indexOf('brand='+aolcss[y])!=-1){return aolcss[y];}
       }
   return false;
 }
 
 function grabUrl() {
    var ticketPath = "http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx/img/sys/exchange/"
    TMObject(mName).SetVariable("serverUrl", ticketPath);
 
    var tmPath = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/"

 }
 
 function starRatingDisplay(rating) {
     var star_rating = (rating - parseInt(rating)).toFixed(1);    var offset;
     switch (star_rating) {
         case "0.1":
              if(parseInt(rating) == 0 || parseInt(rating) == 1){
                  offset = 0;
              }
              else{
                  offset = 1 - parseInt(rating);
              }
              break
         case "0.2": case "0.3":
              offset = 7;
              break
         case "0.4": case "0.5": case "0.6":
              offset = 8;
              break
         case "0.7": case "0.8":
              offset = 9;
              break
         case "0.9":
              if(parseInt(rating) == 0 ){
                  offset = 15;
              }
              else if(parseInt(rating) == 4 ){
                  offset = 14;
              }
              else{
                  offset = 15 - parseInt(rating);
              }
              break
         default:
              if(parseInt(rating) == 1 ){
                  offset = 0;
              }
              else if(parseInt(rating) == 5 ){
                  offset = -1;
              }
              else{
                  offset = 1 - parseInt(rating);
              }
              break
      }
     var final_display_percent = ( parseInt(rating) * 15 +  offset ) + "px";
     return final_display_percent;
  }

 Ajax.Request.prototype.abort = function() {
     this.transport.onreadystatechange = Prototype.emptyFunction;
     this.transport.abort();
     Ajax.activeRequestCount--;
 };
 
 String.prototype.decodeSuggestItem=function() {
     return this.replace(/\&amp\;/g, '\&').replace(/\&gt\;/g, '\>').replace(/\&lt\;/g, '\<').replace(/\&quot\;/g, '\'').replace(/\&\#39\;/g, '\'');
 };
 
 String.prototype.encodeSearchTerm=function(){
     return this.replace(/&/g,"&amp;").replace(/</g,"&lt;").replace(/>/g,"&gt;").replace(/\"/g,"&#34;").replace(/\'/g,"&#39;");
 };
 
 var SearchSuggest = Class.create({
     initialize: function(mode) {
         this.mode = mode !== undefined && mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT ? SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT : SearchSuggest.MODES.STANDARD;
         this.index = 0;
         this.keyword = '';
         this.event = null;
         this.length = 0;
         this.elements = null;
         this.hitMesssage = false;
         this.matchCount = 0;
         this.shownHits = 0;
         this.history = false;
         this.newLocation="";
         this.reset();
         var categories = $$("#search-suggest-categories li");
         for( var i=0; i < categories.length; i++ ) {
             var li = categories[i];
             Event.observe(li, 'mouseover', function () {
                 global.set('cancel_hide', 1);
             });
             Event.observe(li, 'mouseout', function(e) {
                 global.set('cancel_hide', 0);
             });
         }
     },
     _getSuggestCmp: function () {
         return $("search-suggest") || $("searchSuggest");
     },

         search_id.name = "";
         search_id.value = "";
     },

         suggest_header.show();
         this.history = true;
 
         this.hideHitMessage();
         this.showCategories();
         this._getSuggestCmp().show();
     },
     showCategories : function(){
         $('suggest-categories-header').show();
         $('search-suggest-categories').show();
 
         jQuery("#search-suggest-categories li").removeClass("selected");
         this.elements = jQuery(this.elements).add("#search-suggest-categories li");
         this.length = this.elements.length;
     },
     hideCategories : function(){
         this.history = false;
         $('suggest-categories-header').hide();
         $('search-suggest-categories').hide();
     },
     showEmptyHistory: function () {
         this.history = true;
         $('suggest-header').hide();
         this.reset();
         this.hideHitMessage();
         this.showCategories();
         this._getSuggestCmp().show();
     },
     showSuggestionsResults: function () {
         var suggest_header = $('suggest-header');            suggest_header.innerHTML = "Sugerencias";
             suggest_header.show();        this.hideCategories();

     _suggestionEventText: function(upcomingEvents) {
         return upcomingEvents == 1 ?
             " evento" :
             " eventos";
     },
     _buildCircleImage: function(src,circle) {
         var canvas = jQuery('<canvas/>');
         if(circle){
             canvas.addClass('circle');
         }
         canvas = canvas[0];
         canvas.height = 45;
         canvas.width = 45;
 
         var context = canvas.getContext('2d');
         var imageObj = new Image();
         imageObj.onload = function() {
             if(imageObj.width > canvas.width){
                 var imgWidth = imageObj.width;
                 var imgHeight = imageObj.height;
                 var imgOffset = Math.abs(imgWidth - imgHeight)/2;
                 if(imgWidth > imgHeight){
                     context.drawImage(imageObj, imgOffset, 0, imgWidth - imgOffset*2, imgHeight, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                 }else{
                     context.drawImage(imageObj, 0, imgOffset, imgWidth, imgHeight - imgOffset*2, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                 }
             }else{
                 context.drawImage(imageObj, (canvas.width - imageObj.width)/2, (canvas.width - imageObj.width)/2,imageObj.width,imageObj.width);
             }
         };
         imageObj.src = src;
         return canvas;
     },
     buildSuggestionItem: function (params) {
         var item=(typeof params.item=="undefined"?"":params.item);
         var type=(typeof params.type=="undefined"?"":params.type);
         var from=(typeof params.from=="undefined"?"":params.from);
         var pos =(typeof params.pos=="undefined" ? 0:params.pos);
         var link_href, link_target;
         var _parent = this;
         var omnitrack="";
 
         var li = new Element('li', {
              "class": "bucket-item",
              "itemName": (type != "event_exact_match") ? item.name : item.eventName
         });
 
         Event.observe(li, 'mouseover', function () {
             global.set('cancel_hide', 1);
         });
         Event.observe(li, 'mouseout', function(e) {
             global.set('cancel_hide', 0);
         });
 
         var a = jQuery('<a/>');

         a.append(itemWrapperDiv);
         var txtReg=new RegExp($("org_input").value,"gi");
 
         if(typeof item.name !== "undefined"){
             var nameSpan = jQuery('<span/>',{ class: 'name', html: item.name.replace(txtReg, '<strong>$&</strong>')});
             itemTextDiv.append(nameSpan);
         }
         var span = jQuery('<span/>', { class: 'suggest-cat' });
 
         switch (type) {
             case "event_exact_match":
                 omnitrack="SUGG_EDP";
                 itemTextDiv.append(jQuery('<span/>', {
                    class:"bucket-item-highlighted",
                    text: (item.tba) ? "Date TBA" :
                          (item.mdt) ? "Múltiples Fechas y Horarios" :
                          item.date
                 }));
                 if(from=="venue"){
 	               itemTextDiv.append(jQuery('<span/>', {html: item.eventName.replace(txtReg, '<strong>$&</strong>') , class: 'name-venue'}));
 	               itemTextDiv.append(jQuery('<span/>', {
                         html:item.eventSource && item.eventSource == 'tmr' ? item.majorGenre : item.majorGenre+" - "+item.minorGenre,
                         class: 'suggest-cat'
                    }));
                 }else{
 	                itemTextDiv.append(jQuery('<span/>', {html: item.venueName.replace(txtReg, '<strong>$&</strong>'), class: 'name-venue'}));
 	                itemTextDiv.append(jQuery('<span/>', {html: item.eventName.replace(txtReg, '<strong>$&</strong>'), class: 'suggest-cat'}));
 	            }
                 if( item.systemURL !== null){
                      itemTextDiv.append(jQuery('<span/>', {class: 'suggest-cat', html: _parent.getPartnerLocation(item)}));
                 }
                 var event_url_data = _parent.buildEventURL(item);
                 link_href = event_url_data.href;
                 link_target = event_url_data.target;
                 break;
             case "event":
                 omnitrack="SUGG_EDP";
                 jQuery(li).addClass("bucket-item-event");
 
                 span.append(jQuery('<span/>', {
                     class: 'bucket-item-highlighted',
                     html: (item.tba) ? "Date TBA" :
                           (item.mdt) ? "Múltiples Fechas y Horarios" :
                           item.date
                 }));
                 span.append(jQuery('<span/>', {html:item.venueName.replace(txtReg, '<strong>$&</strong>')}));
                 if( item.systemURL !== null){
                      span.append(jQuery('<span/>', {class: 'suggest-cat', html: _parent.getPartnerLocation(item)}));
                 }
                 var event_url_data = _parent.buildEventURL(item);
                 link_href = event_url_data.href;
                 link_target = event_url_data.target;
                 break;
             case "attraction":
                  omnitrack="SUGG_ADP";
                 li.setAttribute('searchId',item.id);
                 li.setAttribute('searchType',"aid");
                 var srcImage;
                 if (item.image == null) {
                     switch (item.majorGenreId[0]) {
                         case 10001 :
                             srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx/img/sys/search/music.png';
                             break;
                         case 10002:
                             srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx/img/sys/search/arts.png';
                             break;
                         case 10003:
                             srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx/img/sys/search/family.png';
                             break;
                         case 10004:
                             srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx/img/sys/search/sports.png';
                             break;
                     }
                 }else{
                     srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx'+item.image;
                 }
                 itemImageDiv.append(_parent._buildCircleImage(srcImage,(item.image == null)?false:true));
                 span.html(item.minorGenreName[0] + ' - ' + item.upcomingEvents + _parent._suggestionEventText(item.upcomingEvents));
                 link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/artist/' + item.id;
                 break;
             case "venue":
                  omnitrack="SUGG_VDP";

                 li.setAttribute('searchType',"vid");
                 var srcImage;
                 if (item.image == null) {
                     srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx/img/sys/search/venue.png';
                 } else {
                     srcImage = 'http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx'+item.image;
                 }
                 itemImageDiv.append(_parent._buildCircleImage(srcImage,(item.image == null)?false:true));
                 span.html (item.venueCityState + ' - ' + item.upcomingEvents + _parent._suggestionEventText(item.upcomingEvents));
                 link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/venue/' + item.id;
                 break;
         }
 
         if (link_href) {
             link_href = _parent.encodedURL(link_href);
             li.setAttribute('data-directURL', link_href);
             a.attr('href', link_href);
             if (link_target) a.attr('target', link_target);
             a.click(function () {
                 if (a.attr('target')) a.attr('href', ga_decorate(a.attr('href')));
                 omniTracking.navigation_link2(omnitrack, {
                     tracking_vars: {
                         eVar7: '' + jQuery('#search_input').val() + ' > ' + item.name + ' (' + omnitrack + ')'
                     }
                 });            });
         }
         li.appendChild(a[0]);
         itemTextDiv.append(span);
         return li;
     },
     buildNewTable: function(data){
         this.reset();
         var suggestion = $("searchSuggest") || $("search-suggest") || $("search-suggest");
 
         var _parent = this;
         if(data.events.length > 0 && data.exactmatches == 0) {
             var event_title = new Element('div', {
                 "class": "search-suggestions-bucket-title"
             });
             event_title.innerHTML = "Próximos eventos cercanos a ti";
             suggestion.appendChild(event_title);
             var events_bucket = new Element('ul', {
                 "class":"absolute-no-bullet select-list-theme search-suggestions-bucket",
                 "id":"events_bucket"
             });
             for( var i = 0; i < data.events.length; i++ ) {
                 events_bucket.appendChild(_parent.buildSuggestionItem({"item":data.events[i],"type":"event","pos": i + 1}));
             }
              if(data.eventsFound && data.eventsFound >= data.events.length && data.events.length==3 ) {
                 events_bucket.appendChild(_parent.getLiSeeMoreItemsFounds({'labelSeeMoreEvents':'Ver más eventos', 'match':false, 'omnitrack':'event'}));
             }
             suggestion.appendChild(events_bucket);
         }
         if(data.attractions.length > 0) {
             var attraction_title = new Element('div', {
                 "class": "search-suggestions-bucket-title bordered"
             });
             attraction_title.innerHTML = "Artistas";
             suggestion.appendChild(attraction_title);
             var attractions_bucket = new Element('ul', {
                 "class":"absolute-no-bullet select-list-theme search-suggestions-bucket",
                 "id":"attractions_bucket"
             });
 
             for( var i = 0; i < data.attractions.length; i++ ) {
                 var attraction = data.attractions[i];
                 attractions_bucket.appendChild(_parent.buildSuggestionItem({"item":attraction,"type":"attraction","pos": i+ 1}));
 
                 for(var j = 0; j < attraction.events.length; j ++){
                     attractions_bucket.appendChild(_parent.buildSuggestionItem({"item":attraction.events[j],"type":"event_exact_match","from":"attraction","pos": j + 1}));
                 }
 
                 if(attraction.upcomingEvents >= attraction.events.length && attraction.events.length == 3) {
                     attractions_bucket.appendChild(
                         _parent.getLiSeeMoreItemsFounds({'labelSeeMoreEvents':'Ver más eventos', 'match':true, 'type':'attraction', 'item':attraction, 'omnitrack':'attraction'})
                     );
                 }
             }
             if(data.attractionsFound && data.attractionsFound > data.attractions.length) {
                 var li=_parent.getLiSeeMoreItemsFounds({'labelSeeMoreEvents':'Ver Más Artistas', 'match':false, 'omnitrack':'attraction'});
                 attractions_bucket.appendChild(li);
             }
             suggestion.appendChild(attractions_bucket);
         }
         if(data.venues.length > 0) {
             var venues_title = new Element('div', {
                 "class": "search-suggestions-bucket-title bordered"
             });
             venues_title.innerHTML = "Lugares de eventos";
             suggestion.appendChild(venues_title);
             var venues_bucket = new Element('ul', {
                 "class":"absolute-no-bullet select-list-theme search-suggestions-bucket",
                 "id":"venues_bucket"
             });
             for( var i = 0; i < data.venues.length; i++ ) {
               var venue = data.venues[i];
               venues_bucket.appendChild(_parent.buildSuggestionItem({"item":venue,"type":"venue","pos":i+1}));
 
               for(var j = 0; j < venue.events.length; j ++){
                   venues_bucket.appendChild(_parent.buildSuggestionItem({"item":venue.events[j],"type":"event_exact_match","from":"venue","pos": j + 1}));
               }
 
               if(venue.upcomingEvents >= venue.events.length && venue.events.length == 3) {
                   venues_bucket.appendChild(
                       _parent.getLiSeeMoreItemsFounds( {'labelSeeMoreEvents':'Ver más eventos', 'match':true, 'type':'venue', 'item':venue, 'omnitrack':'venue'} )
                   );
               }
             }
             if(data.venuesFound && data.venuesFound > data.venues.length) {
                 venues_bucket.appendChild(_parent.getLiSeeMoreItemsFounds({'labelSeeMoreEvents':'Ver Más Lugares de Eventos', 'match':false, 'omnitrack':'venue'}));
             }
             suggestion.appendChild(venues_bucket);
         }
         this.elements = jQuery('.bucket-item');
         this.length = this.elements.length;
         this.showSuggestionsResults();
     },
 
     buildEventURL: function(event){
         var event_url, target;
 
         if( event.PostProcessedData && event.PostProcessedData.system_url ) {
             var current_domain = 'mx';
             var valid_partner = false;
             if (event.purchase_domain) {
                 valid_partner = true;
             } else {
                 var url = event.systemURL.toLowerCase();
                 if (url) {
                     var queue;
                     if (current_domain == 'au') {
                         queue = ['ticketing.ticketmaster.com.au'];
                     } else if (current_domain == 'us' || current_domain == 'ca') {
                         queue = ['ticketweb'];
                     } else {
                         queue = tm_omni_temp.get(current_domain + '_h');
                     }
                     if (queue) {
                         for (i = 0 ; i < queue.length ; i++) {
                             if (url.indexOf(queue[i]) !== -1) {
                                 valid_partner = true;
                                 break;
                             }
                         }
                     }
                 }
             }
             var pr_postpend = "&eventid=" + event.id + "&artistid=" + event.AttractionId.first();
 
             if (valid_partner) {
                pr_postpend += "&crosssite=TM_MX:" + event.AttractionId.first() + ":" + event.venueId;
             }
             event_url = 'http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/partner_redirect?v=' + encodeURIComponent( event.PostProcessedData.system_url ) + pr_postpend;
             target = '_blank';
 
             if( event.eventSource && event.eventSource == 'tmr' ){
                 target = '';
             }
 
         }
         else {
             event_url = 'http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/' + event.SEOName + '/event/' + event.id + '?artistid=' + event.AttractionId.first();
             target = '';
         }        if (event.id.indexOf('ticketweb-') !== -1) {
             var ccpEdpHost = 'www1.ticketmaster.com.mx';
             var newUrl = ccpEdpHost + '/event/'+ event.id;
             //Use this element to parse the url and get the original protocol
             var parser = document.createElement('a');
             parser.href = event_url;
             event_url = parser.protocol + '//' + newUrl;
             target = '';
         }        return {href: event_url, target: target} ;
     },
 
     getPartnerLocation : function (event) {
         var disp_hop_text = '';
         var org_hash = {
             'other' : {
                  org_id : 14,
                 hop_txt : 'en sitio asociado'
             },12 : {
                  org_id : 11,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },1 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },2 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },3 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },4 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },5 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },6 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },7 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },8 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },9 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },10 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             },11 : {
                  org_id : 12,
                 hop_txt : ''
             }        };
         if (event.systemURL) {
             var is_resalePartner = check_resalePartnerURL( event.systemURL );
             if(event.PurchaseDomain){
                 if (is_resalePartner) {
                     disp_hop_text = 'Resale Tickets on Partner Site';
                 }else{
                     disp_hop_text = org_hash[ event.PurchaseDomain ].hop_txt;
                 }
             }else {
                 if (is_resalePartner) {
                     disp_hop_text = 'Resale Tickets on Partner Site';
                 }else{
                     if (event.PostProcessedData.PollingLinkStatus == '1'){
                         disp_hop_text = event.PostProcessedData.PollingLinkText;
                     }else {
                         disp_hop_text = org_hash[ 'other' ].hop_txt;
                     }
                 }
             }
         }
         if (event.PostProcessedData && event.PostProcessedData.PollingLinkStatus == '2'){
             disp_hop_text = "";
         }
         return disp_hop_text;
     },
 
     encodedURL: function(link_href){
         var parsed_uri,parsed_query;
         parsed_uri = __GLOBALS.util.parseURI(link_href);
         if (parsed_uri) {
             parsed_query = __GLOBALS.util.parseAndDecodeURIQuery(parsed_uri.query);
             if (!parsed_query) {
                 parsed_query = {};
             }
             parsed_query.tm_link = "tm_homeA_header_search";
             parsed_uri.query = __GLOBALS.util.encodeAndBuildURIQuery(parsed_query);
             link_href = __GLOBALS.util.buildURI(parsed_uri);
         }
         return link_href;
     },
     /*
     * {labelSeeMoreEvents, match, type, item, omnitrack}
     */
     getLiSeeMoreItemsFounds: function (params) {
 
          var labelSeeMoreEvents=params.labelSeeMoreEvents;
          var match=params.match;
          var type=params.type;
          var item=params.item;
          var omnitrack=params.omnitrack;
          var _parent = this;
          var li = jQuery('<li/>', {class: "bucket-item", itemName: _parent.keyword});
 
          Event.observe(li[0], 'mouseover', function () {
              global.set('cancel_hide', 1);
          });
          Event.observe(li[0], 'mouseout', function (e) {
              global.set('cancel_hide', 0);
          });
 
          var a = jQuery('<a/>', { class: "bucket-item-highlighted"});
          var itemWrapperDiv = jQuery('<div/>', {class: 'bucket-item-wrapper'});
          var itemImageDiv = jQuery('<div/>', {class: 'bucket-item-image'});
          var itemTextDiv = jQuery('<div/>', {class: 'bucket-item-text'});
          itemWrapperDiv.append(itemImageDiv, itemTextDiv);
          a.append(itemWrapperDiv);
 
          var nameSpan = jQuery('<span/>', {html: labelSeeMoreEvents});
          var link_href;
          itemTextDiv.append(nameSpan);
          var omnitrackTag="";
           switch (omnitrack) {
               case "attraction" :
                   omnitrackTag = "SUGG_MORE_PERFORMERS";
                   break;
                case "event" :
                   omnitrackTag = "SUGG_MORE_EVENTS";
                   break;
               case "venue" :
                   omnitrackTag = "SUGG_MORE_VENUES";
                   break;
             }
           if(omnitrackTag!=""){
               a.click(function(){
                 omniTracking.navigation_link2(omnitrackTag, {
                    tracking_vars: {
                       eVar7: ''+ jQuery('#search_input').val()+' ('+omnitrackTag+')'
                       }
                   });              });
             }
          li.append(a);
          if (!match) {
             itemTextDiv.addClass('more-items');
             Event.observe(li[0], 'click', function (e) {
                 _parent.updateHiddenId(this);
                 e.stop();
                 $('search_form').submit();
             });
          }else{
             switch (type) {
                 case "attraction" :
                     link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/artist/' + item.id;
                     break;
                 case "venue" :
                     link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/venue/' + item.id;
                     break;
             }
             link_href = _parent.encodedURL(link_href);
             li.attr('data-directURL', link_href);
             a.attr('href',link_href);
          }
          return li[0];
      },
 
     buildTable: function(data) {
         this.reset();
         var suggest_ul = $("searchSuggest-result");
         var _parent = this;
         var link_href;
         var parsed_uri,
             parsed_query;
         var dataItem;
         for( var i=0; i < 10 && i < data.length; i++ ) {
             dataItem = data[i];
             var search_type = dataItem.VenueId ? "vid" : "aid";
             var search_id = dataItem.AttractionId ? dataItem.AttractionId[0] : dataItem.VenueId;
             var item_name = dataItem.Autocomplete;
             var li = new Element('li', {
                 "li_index": i,
                 "searchType": search_type,
                 "searchId": search_id,
                 "itemName": item_name
             });
             Event.observe(li, 'mouseover', function () {
                 global.set('cancel_hide', 1);
                 _parent.updateTable(this);
             });
             Event.observe(li, 'mouseout', function(e) {
                 global.set('cancel_hide', 0);
                 this.className = "";
             });
             Event.observe(li, 'click', function(e) {
                 var query = jQuery('#search_input').val();
                 _parent.updateHiddenId(this);                if ( _parent.mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.STANDARD ) {
                   e.stop();
                   $('search_form').submit();
                 }
             });
 
             var event_count = dataItem.UpcomingEvents + " eventos";
             var follow_span = new Element('span', {"class":"suggest-cat"});
             if ( dataItem.VenueId ) {
                 var venue_follow_str = dataItem.CityState;
                     venue_follow_str = venue_follow_str + " - " + event_count;                follow_span.innerHTML = "(" + venue_follow_str + ")";
             }
             else if (dataItem.AttractionId){
 
                 var major_cate = dataItem.MainMajorGenre;
                 var minor_cate = dataItem.MainMinorGenre;
                 var major_id = dataItem.MajorGenreId[0];
                 var arr_str = new Array();
                 var tmp_str;
                 //control Search Suggest display by combination of Domian & Major Cat
                 switch (major_id) {
                     //music
                     case 10001 :
                         arr_str.push(major_cate);
                         arr_str.push(minor_cate);
                         arr_str.push(event_count);                        break;
                     //art&theater
                     case 10002 :
                         arr_str.push(major_cate);
                         arr_str.push(minor_cate);
                         arr_str.push(event_count);                        break;
                     //family
                     case 10003 :
                         arr_str.push(major_cate);
                         arr_str.push(minor_cate);
                         arr_str.push(event_count);                        break;
                     //sports
                     case 10004 :
                         arr_str.push(major_cate);
                         arr_str.push(minor_cate);
                         arr_str.push(event_count);                        break;
                     default :
                         break;
                 }
 
                 if ( arr_str.length > 0) {
                     tmp_str = arr_str.join(" - ");
                     follow_span.innerHTML = "(" + tmp_str + ")";
                 }
             }
             var a = new Element('a');
             a.innerHTML = dataItem.AutocompleteHighlight;
             if (this.mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT) {
                 link_href = undefined;
                 if (dataItem.VenueId) {
                     link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/venue/' + dataItem.VenueId;
                 } else if (dataItem.AttractionId && dataItem.AttractionId) {
                     link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/artist/' + dataItem.AttractionId;
                 }
                 if (link_href) {
                     link_href = _parent.encodedURL(link_href);
                     li.setAttribute('data-directURL', link_href);
                     a.href = link_href;
                 }
             }
             a.appendChild(follow_span);
             li.appendChild(a);
             suggest_ul.insert(li);
         }
         var suggest = $("search-suggest") || $("searchSuggest");
         Event.observe(suggest, 'mouseout', function(e) {
             this.index = -1;
         });
         this.elements = $$("#searchSuggest-result li");
         this.length = this.elements.length;
         this.showSuggestionsResults();
     },
     getData: function() {
         var _parent = this;
         var time;
         var opt = {
             method: "get",
             onCreate : function(){
                 time = new Date().getTime()
             },
             onSuccess: function(t) {
                 var data;
                 if(t.responseText)
                     data = t.responseText.evalJSON(true);
                 _parent._getSuggestCmp().hide();
                 if (data && data.events && data.events.length && sortEventByTbaDateName) {
                     data.events.sort(sortEventByTbaDateName);
                 }                if (data.response && data.response.docs.length > 0) {
                     _parent.shownHits = data.response.docs.length;
                     _parent.matchCount = data.response.numFound;
                     _parent.buildTable(data.response.docs);
                 }            },
             onFailure: function() {
                 alert("An error occurred, please try again later.");
             }
         };
         var prev_ajax = global.get('myajax');
         if ( prev_ajax ) {
             prev_ajax.abort();
         }
         var requestURL = 'http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/json/search/suggest?q=' + encodeURIComponent(this.keyword) ;
 
         if( typeof search_suggest_a_b !== "undefined" ){
             requestURL += '&nsse=' + search_suggest_a_b;
         }
 
         if (typeof search_suggest_by_market_a_b !== "undefined") {
             requestURL += '&nssmid=' + search_suggest_by_market_a_b;
         }
 
         if(_parent.useDisco() || (typeof force_use_disco !== "undefined" && force_use_disco)){
             requestURL += '&ud=y';
         }
 
         var market_id = GetCookie("MARKET_ID");
         if( market_id ) {
             requestURL += '&market_id=' + market_id;
         }
 
         var curr_ajax = new Ajax.Request(requestURL, opt);
         global.set('myajax', curr_ajax);
     },
     updateTable: function(li) {
         if ( this.index >= 0 ) {
             this.elements[this.index].className = "";
         }
         li.className = "selected";
         this.index = li.getAttribute('li_index');
     },
     updateHiddenId: function(li) {
         var search_type = li.getAttribute('searchType');
         var search_id = li.getAttribute('searchId');
         var item_name = li.getAttribute('itemName');
         $("search_input").value = item_name.decodeSuggestItem();
         if(search_id) {
             var search_id_element = $('search_id');
             search_id_element.name = search_type;
             search_id_element.value = search_id;
         }
     },
     autoComplete: function (keyword) {
         this.keyword = keyword;
         this.getData();
     },
     showSearchHistory: function(){
         var _parent = this;
         var searches;
         try{
             searches = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(TMCookie.get('TM_SEARCH_HISTORY')));
         }catch(e){
             searches = [];
         }
         var link_href;
         var parsed_uri,parsed_query;
         if (searches && searches.constructor === Array && searches.length > 0) {
             this.reset();
             var suggest_ul = $("searchSuggest-result");
             var dataItem;
             for (var i = 0; i < searches.length; i++) {
                 dataItem = searches[i];
                 var item_name = dataItem.search.replace(/\+/g," ");
                 var li = new Element('li', {
                     "li_index": i,
                     "itemName": item_name,
                     "class": "recent"
                 });
                 var a = new Element('a');
                 a.innerHTML = item_name;
 
                 Event.observe(li, 'mouseover', function () {
                     global.set('cancel_hide', 1);
                 });
                 Event.observe(li, 'mouseout', function(e) {
                     global.set('cancel_hide', 0);
                 });
 
                 Event.observe(li, 'click', function (e) {
                      omniTracking.navigation_link2('SUGG_HIST',{
                       tracking_vars: {
                          eVar7:  item_name + ' (SUGG_HIST)'
                       }
                     });
                     _parent.updateHiddenId(this);
                     if (_parent.mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.STANDARD) {
                         e.stop();
                         $("org_input").value = item_name;
                         $('search_form').submit();
                     }
                 });
 
                 if (this.mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT) {
 
                     link_href = "http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx" + '/search?q='+dataItem.search;
                     parsed_uri = __GLOBALS.util.parseURI(link_href);
                     if (parsed_uri) {
                         parsed_query = __GLOBALS.util.parseAndDecodeURIQuery(parsed_uri.query);
                         if (!parsed_query) {
                             parsed_query = {};
                         }
                         parsed_query.tm_link = "tm_homeA_header_search";
                         parsed_uri.query = __GLOBALS.util.encodeAndBuildURIQuery(parsed_query);
                         link_href = __GLOBALS.util.buildURI(parsed_uri);
                     }
                     li.setAttribute('data-directURL', link_href);
                     a.href = link_href;
                 }
                 li.appendChild(a);
                 suggest_ul.insert(li);
             }
             this.elements = $$("#searchSuggest-result li");
             this.length = this.elements.length;
             this.showHistory();
         } else {
             this.showEmptyHistory();
         }
     },
     prev: function() {
         if ( this.elements ) {
             if ( this.index > 0 ) {
                 this.elements[this.index].className = "";
                 this.index--;
                 this.elements[this.index].className = "selected";
                 this.updateHiddenId(this.elements[this.index]);
             }
             else {
                 this.index = -1;
                 initHiddenParam();
                 this.elements[0].className = "";
                 $("search_input").value = $("org_input").value;
             }
         }
     },
     next: function() {
         if ( this.elements ) {
             if ( this.index >= 0 ) {
                 this.elements[this.index].className = "";
             }
             this.index = (++this.index) % this.length;
             this.elements[this.index].className = "selected";
             this.updateHiddenId(this.elements[this.index]);
         }
     },
     currentElement: function () {
         return this.elements && this.elements[this.index] ? this.elements[this.index] : null;
     },
 
     /*new search suggestions functions*/
     pressEnter: function(event) {
         if(this.elements != null && ((jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).attr('data-directURL') != ""
                 && typeof jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).attr('data-directURL') != "undefined")
                 ||
             jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).is("#search-suggest-categories li"))
         ){
 			jQuery("a", this.elements[this.index]).get(0).click();
         }else{
 			jQuery("#search_form").submit();
 		}
     },
     prev_new: function() {
         if (this.elements) {
             if (this.index > 0) {
                 jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).removeClass("selected");
                 this.index--;
                 jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).addClass("selected");
                 if (jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).is("#search-suggest-categories li")) {
                     $("search_input").value = "";
                 }
                 else {
                     this.updateHiddenId(this.elements[this.index]);
                 }
             }
             else {
                 this.index = -1;
                 initHiddenParam();
                 jQuery(this.elements[0]).removeClass("selected");
                 $("search_input").value = $("org_input").value;
             }
         }
     },
     next_new: function() {
         if (this.elements) {
             if (this.index >= 0) {
                 jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).removeClass("selected");
             }
             this.index = (++this.index) % this.length;
             jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).addClass("selected");
             if (jQuery(this.elements[this.index]).is("#search-suggest-categories li")) {
                 $("search_input").value = "";
             }
             else {
                 this.updateHiddenId(this.elements[this.index]);
             }
         }
     },
     showHitMessage: function () {
         this.hitMesssage = true;
         $('suggest-tip-message').show();
         $('suggest-header').hide();
         this.hideCategories();
         this.reset();
         this._getSuggestCmp().show();
     },
     hideHitMessage : function () {
         this.hitMesssage = false;
         $('suggest-tip-message').hide();
     },    useDisco : function(){
         try {
             var query_params = $H(window.location.search.toQueryParams());
             if( query_params.get('ud') === 'y'){
                 return true;
             }
         }
         catch (e) {}
         return false;
     }
 });
 
 SearchSuggest.MODES = {
     STANDARD: "standardMode",
     DIRECT: "directMode"
 };
 
 SearchSuggest.DISPLAY = {
     NONE: 0,
     LEGACY: 1,
     NEW: 2
 };
 
 function showSearchHistory(event) {
     var keyword = $("search_input").value;
     if(keyword.length == 0){              searchHistory.delay("0.1");    }
 }
 function showNewSuggestions() {
     var event = arguments[0] || event;
     var search_input = $("search_input");
     var keyword = search_input.value;
     var suggestion = $("searchSuggest") || $("search-suggest") || $("search-suggest");
 
     if (keyword.length == 0 && ( search_suggest.hitMesssage || suggestion.style.display === 'none')) {
         $("org_input").value = keyword;
         searchHistory.delay("0.1");
     }
     else if(keyword.length > 0 && keyword.length < 3) {
         $("org_input").value = keyword;
 
         if (!processKey(event) && !search_suggest.hitMesssage) {
             suggestion.hide();
             searchHitMessage.delay("0.1")
         }
         var exist_ajax = global.get('myajax');
         if (exist_ajax) {
             exist_ajax.abort();
         }
 
     } else {
         if (!processKey(event)) {
             $("org_input").value = keyword;
             sendRequest.delay("0.1", keyword);
         }
     }
 }
 
 function processKey(event) {
     switch (event.keyCode) {
         case KEY.UP:
             search_suggest.prev_new();
             return true;
         case KEY.DOWN:
             search_suggest.next_new();
             return true;
         case KEY.ESC:
             search_suggest.reset();
             search_input.value = $("org_input").value;
             return true;
         case KEY.ENTER:
             search_suggest.pressEnter(event);
             return true;
     }
 
     return false;
 }
 
 function showSuggestions() {
     var event = arguments[0] || event;
     var keyword = $("search_input").value;
     var suggestion = $("searchSuggest") || $("search-suggest") || $("search-suggest");
     if(keyword.length < 3){
         $("org_input").value = keyword;
         var exist_ajax = global.get('myajax');
         if ( exist_ajax ) {
             exist_ajax.abort();
         }
     }
     if(keyword.length == 0){
         suggestion.hide();
         search_suggest.hideHitMessage();
     }
     else if(keyword.length > 0 && keyword.length < 3) {
         if(!search_suggest.hitMesssage) {
             suggestion.hide();
             searchHitMessage.delay("0.1")
         }
         if (event.keyCode  == KEY.ENTER) {
             search_suggest.pressEnter(event);
         }
     }
     else {
         switch (event.keyCode) {
                 case KEY.UP:
                     search_suggest.prev();
                     break;
                 case KEY.DOWN:
                     search_suggest.next();
                     break;
                 case KEY.ESC:
                     search_suggest.reset();
                     $("search_input").value = $("org_input").value;
                     break;
                 case KEY.ENTER:
                     break;
                 default:
                     $("org_input").value = keyword;
                     sendRequest.delay("0.1", keyword);
                     break;
         }
     }
 }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var check_resalePartnerURL;
 (function () {
     var resale_disclaimer_config = { partners: null };
     check_resalePartnerURL = function (url) {
         if ( !resale_disclaimer_config.partners || !url || typeof url !== 'string' ) {
             return false;
         }
         var result = __GLOBALS.util.parseURI(url);
         if (!result || !result.host) {
             return false;
         }
         var result_host_lowercase = result.host.replace(/\s*$/, '').toLowerCase();
         var i,
             key,
             values;
         for (key in resale_disclaimer_config.partners) {
             values = resale_disclaimer_config.partners[key].hosts;
             if (!values) {
                 continue;
             }
             for (i = 0 ; i < values.length ; i++) {
                 if (values[i].toLowerCase() === result_host_lowercase) {
                     return true;
                 }
             }
         }
         return false;
     };
 })();
 
 function ga_decorate(url){
     var gobj = window[window.GoogleAnalyticsObject];
     if (gobj) {
         var tracker = gobj.getAll()[0];
         if (tracker) {
             var linker = new window.gaplugins.Linker(tracker);
             if (linker) {
                 url = linker.decorate (url);
             }
         }
     }
     return url;
 }

       var reg_ex = new RegExp("&eacute;","g");
     var replaceItem = '\u00E9';
 
 var search_text = "Qué estás buscando?";
 search_text = search_text.replace(reg_ex,replaceItem);
 
 function checkSearchFormAction(form) {
     var current_suggest = typeof search_suggest !== 'undefined' && search_suggest ? search_suggest.currentElement() : null;
     if (typeof search_suggest !== 'undefined' && search_suggest && search_suggest.mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT && current_suggest && current_suggest.getAttribute('data-directURL')) {
         window.location = current_suggest.getAttribute('data-directURL');
         return false;
     } else {
         return verifySearchString(form);
     }
 }
 
 function verifySearchString(form) {
     if(form.q.value.replace(/^\s*|\s*$/g,'') == "" || form.q.value == search_text ){
         /* Avoid the alert validation on empty keyword search when a category item is selected by keyboard. */
         alert(checkUni("Escribe el texto para la búsqueda."));
         form.q.focus();
         form.q.value = "";
         return false;
     }
     if (typeof(edp) != "undefined" && edp !== null && edp.active_mode == 'isc' && edp.isc.cart.items.length) {
         return edp.isc.cart.leaving_isc_dialog.on_form_submit_attempt(form);
     }
     return true;
 }
 
 function createSearchSuggestion(isSuperNavMiniSearch) {
 
     search_suggest = search_suggest || new SearchSuggest( typeof searchSuggest_direct !== 'undefined' && searchSuggest_direct ? SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT : SearchSuggest.MODES.STANDARD );
         var keyup= function(event){                showSuggestions(event);        };      var msie = !(window.ActiveXObject) && "ActiveXObject" in window
       if (msie==true) { // If Internet Explorer
       document.getElementById('search_input').onkeypress = keyup;
       }
       document.getElementById('search_input').onkeyup = keyup;
     Event.observe($('search_input'), 'blur', function(event) {
         if ( this.value == '' ) {
             this.value = search_text;
             this.style.color ='#898989';
         }        if ( global.get('cancel_hide') == 0 ) {
             var suggest = $("search-suggest") || $("searchSuggest") || $("search-suggest");
             if(suggest){
                 suggest.hide();
             }
             $("searchSuggest-result").update('');
             if (search_suggest.mode === SearchSuggest.MODES.DIRECT) {
                 search_suggest.reset();
             }
             updateInputText(this);
         }
     });
 };

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function getEvents( idList, listType ) {
         var param = listType + '=' + idList;
         var opt = {
             method: 'get',
             parameters: param,
             onSuccess: function(t) {
                 var data = t.responseText.evalJSON(true).facet_counts.facet_fields;
                     data = listType == 'vid' ? data.VenueId : data.AttractionId;
                 var prefix = listType == 'vid' ? 'v_' : 'a_';
                 var p_list = data.partition( function(a){ return Object.isString( a ) });
                 var data_id = p_list[0];
                 var data_count = p_list[1];
                 for( var i = 0 ; i < data_id.length ; i++ ) {
                   if($(prefix + data_id[i] + '_events')){
                     $(prefix + data_id[i] + '_events').innerHTML = listType == 'vid' ? data_count[i] : ((data_count[i] == 1) ? data_count[i] + ' evento' : data_count[i] + ' eventos');
                   }
                 }
             },
             onFailure: function() {
                 if(listType == "vid"){
                   vidh = ((vids.size > 0 ) ? vids : local_venue_ids);
                     vidh.each( function(c){
                     if ($('v_' + c + '_events')){
                         $('v_' + c + '_events').hide();
                     }
                     if ($('v_' + c + '_events_vid')){
                         $('v_' + c + '_events_vid').hide();
                     }
                     });
                 }
             }
         }
         new Ajax.Request('http://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/json/search/event/count', opt);
     }
       </script>

          <script language="javascript">
           function check_for_range2(form){
  if (form.rdc_select.options[form.rdc_select.selectedIndex].value == "range") {
     if(document.browse['area'].value.indexOf(checkUni("Ciudad o código postal"))!=-1){
        document.browse['area'].value="";
        }
   // logic for calculating current date + 7 days
   rday = cday + 7;
   rmonth = cmonth;
   ryear = cyear;
 
   days_in_month = dim(rmonth, ryear);
 
   if ((rday) > days_in_month) {
    rday = rday - days_in_month;
    if (rmonth + 1 > 12) {
     ryear += 1;
     rmonth = 1;
    }
    else rmonth += 1;
   }
 
   rcat = form.category.options[form.category.selectedIndex].value;
   rarea = escape(form.area.value);
   // loads range page with todays date and date + 7
   if(document.browse.teVal){
   document.location = "/exchange/buy/browse?category=" + rcat + "&area=" + rarea + "&rdc_syear=" + cyear + "&rdc_smonth=" + cmonth + "&rdc_sday=" + cday + "&rdc_eyear=" + ryear + "&rdc_emonth=" + rmonth + "&rdc_eday=" + rday + "&type=range";
      }else{
   document.location = "/browse?category=" + rcat + "&tm_link=tm_home_browse&area=" + rarea + "&rdc_syear=" + cyear + "&rdc_smonth=" + cmonth + "&rdc_sday=" + cday + "&rdc_eyear=" + ryear + "&rdc_emonth=" + rmonth + "&rdc_eday=" + rday + "&type=range";
    }
  }
 } // check for range
          </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         var minor = null;
 new OnWindowLoad( function() {
 if($('minor_cat_dropdown')) {
     minor = jQuery("#minor_cat_dropdown").tmDropdown({
         auto_width: false,
         rows: 10,
         adjustScrollbarWidth: rebranding_mvp,
         adjustContentWidth: rebranding_mvp,
         on_change: function() {
             if($('category')) { 
                 $('category').value = jQuery("#minor_cat_dropdown").tmDropdown( 'get_value' );
             }
         }
     });
     jQuery("#minor_cat_dropdown").tmDropdown( 'disable' );
 
 }
 
 if($('major_cat_dropdown')) {
     function on_major_cat_change( dropdown ) {
         var major_cat_id = dropdown.get_value();
 
         $('root').value = major_cat_id;
         
         var h = $H(genres[major_cat_id]);
         
         if(h.any()) {
             // clear out all options but index 0
             var options = minor.tmDropdown( 'get_all_options' );
             for ( var i = 1 ; i < options.length; i ++ ) {
                 minor.tmDropdown( 'remove_option', jQuery(options[i]) );
             }
 
             // add new options from h
             h.each( function( pair ) {
                 minor.tmDropdown( 'add_option', pair[1], pair[0] );
             });
 
             if($('category')) {
 		$('category').value = major_cat_id;
 	    }
 
             minor.tmDropdown( 'enable' );
         }
         else {
             minor
                 .tmDropdown( 'select_option_by_index', 0 )
                 .tmDropdown( 'disable' );
             
             $('category').value = 'NULL';
         }
     }
 
     jQuery("#major_cat_dropdown").tmDropdown({
         rows: 10,
         auto_width: false,
         on_change: on_major_cat_change,
         adjustScrollbarWidth: rebranding_mvp,
         adjustContentWidth: rebranding_mvp
     });
 }
 
 if($('rdc_select_drop')) {
     function on_rdc_select_change ( dropdown ) {
         var value = jQuery("#rdc_select_drop").tmDropdown( 'get_value' );
         $('rdc_select').value = value;
         if( value == 'range' ) {
             buildCalendarPicker(); 
             $('browse_calendar_picker').show();
         } else {
             $('browse_calendar_picker').hide();
         }
     };
 
     jQuery("#rdc_select_drop").tmDropdown({
         rows: 10,
         auto_width: false,
         on_change: on_rdc_select_change,
         adjustScrollbarWidth: rebranding_mvp,
         adjustContentWidth: rebranding_mvp
     });
 
     on_rdc_select_change();
 }
 
 });
        </script>

         <script language="JavaScript">
          var tmlink_count = 1;
         var xmlDisplay = ""
   var prevPos = 0;
   var pos = 0;
   var slots = 4;
   var highestCounter = slots + 1;
   var isAnimating = false; 
   var fromPrevOrNext = false;
         var firstRun = false;
   var rs_countdown;
         var maxbtn = 4;
   //CHECK FOR IE6
   function is_ie6(){ return ((window.XMLHttpRequest == undefined) && (ActiveXObject != undefined)); }
   function rs_choose(i, override) {
     if (!fromPrevOrNext){
       prevPos = pos;
     }
     if ( ( pos != i-1 || override ) && !isAnimating ) {     
       //reset 
       $$("#spotlight-buttons li").each(function(btn){
         btn.removeClassName("selected");  
       });
                 if(firstRun == false){
                     firstRun = true;
                    }
       pos = i-1;
       $$("#list-spotlight li").each(function(s){ s.style.zIndex = highestCounter-2;  });
       $$("#list-spotlight li")[prevPos].style.zIndex = highestCounter-1;
       $$("#list-spotlight li")[pos].style.zIndex = highestCounter;
       $$("#list-spotlight li")[pos].hide();      $$("#list-spotlight .shade-module")[prevPos].slideUp( {
       duration:0.3,
       beforeSetup:function(){ 
         isAnimating = true;         
              },
       afterFinish:function(){       
         shadeFilters("disable");
         $$("#list-spotlight li")[pos].appear({
             duration:0.5,
             afterFinish: function(){              
               $$("#list-spotlight .shade-module")[pos].slideDown( {       
                   duration:0.3, 
                   beforeSetup:function() { 
                     shadeFilters();                   
                   },
                   afterFinish:function() { 
                     isAnimating = false; 
                     fromPrevOrNext = false;
                   }             
                 }
               );          
             }           
           }
         );        
       }
     });                     if($$("#spotlight-buttons li")[pos]){
       $$("#spotlight-buttons li")[pos].addClassName("selected");
                      }
       sendSpotlightViewPixel(); 
     }
   }
   
   function shadeFilters(option) {
     if (is_ie6()) {
       //alert("IE 6 Mode");
       var shade = $$("#list-spotlight .shade-module b");
       if (option == "disable") {
         for (i=0; i<shade.length; i++){
           shade[i].style.filter = "none";
         }
       }
       else {
         for (i=0; i<shade.length; i++){
           shade[i].style.filter = "alpha(opacity=75)";
         }
       }
     }
   }
   
   function rs_next() {  
     fromPrevOrNext = true;
     if (!isAnimating) {
       prevPos = pos;
       pos++;
       if(pos > slots-1) {
         pos = 0
         rs_choose(pos+1, true); 
       }
       else { 
         rs_choose(pos+1, true);
       }
       
     }
   }
   
   function rs_prev() {  
     fromPrevOrNext = true;
     if(!isAnimating) {
       prevPos = pos;
       pos--;
       if(pos < 0) {
         pos = slots-1;
         rs_choose(pos+1, true);
       }
       else {
         rs_choose(pos+1, true);
       }
     }
   }
 
 
   $$(".shade-module").invoke('hide');
         $$(".shade-module")[0].show();  function rs_countdown_init() {  
     rs_countdown = setTimeout( function(){ 
       rs_next(); 
       rs_countdown_init(); 
     }, 7000);
   }
 
   function rs_countdown_clear() { clearTimeout(rs_countdown); }
   function rs_remove_blur() { jQuery("#spotLite").undelegate("a", "blur"); }
 
   function rs_countdown_clear_on_focus () {
       var block_on_focus = false;
       
       jQuery("#spotLite").delegate("a", "focus", function () {
           if (!block_on_focus) {
               block_on_focus = true; 
               rs_countdown_clear();
           } 
       }).delegate("a", "blur", function (){
           rs_get_active(function () {
               if (jQuery(document.activeElement) == jQuery("body") || !jQuery(document.activeElement).closest("#spotLite").length){
                   block_on_focus = false;
                   rs_countdown_init(); 
               }
           }, 0);
       }); 
 
   };
 
   function rs_get_active (callback, time){
       setTimeout(callback, time);
   };
 
   function sendSpotlightViewPixel()
   {
     var slot         = pos + 1;
     var scheduleId   = jQuery('#spotlightentry' + slot).attr('data-storyid');
     var scheduleSlot = jQuery('#spotlightentry' + slot).attr('data-slot');
     var data         = { data : scheduleSlot + '|' + scheduleId };
     window.TM.audienceSolutions = window.TM.audienceSolutions || [];
     window.TM.audienceSolutions.push(['sptLght_view', data]);
   }
 
         sendSpotlightViewPixel(); // sending spotlight view pixel for the first slot (when page loads), before slot button click or rotation occurs.
 
         rs_countdown_init();
         rs_countdown_clear_on_focus();
            
                 
                      
 
                         $("rs-btn1").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_choose(1);} ); 
                      
 
                         $("rs-btn2").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_choose(2);} ); 
                      
 
                         $("rs-btn3").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_choose(3);} ); 
                      
 
                         $("rs-btn4").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_choose(4);} ); 
                      
                    
 
                              $("rs-prev").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_prev();} );
                              $("rs-next").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_next();} );
                              $("rs-pause").observe("click", function(){rs_countdown_clear(); rs_remove_blur(); });
         </script>

         <div id="onSaleWrap">
          <ul id="js-onsale-tab" role="tablist" style="list-style-type:none;padding:0px">
           <li aria-controls="onsale_now_data" aria-selected="true" class="now_on text-indent" data-activeclass="now_on" data-disabledclass="now" data-omn="salenow" id="onsale_now_tab" role="tab" style="display:inline;" tabindex="0">
            Compra hoy
           </li>
           <li aria-controls="onsale_soon_data" aria-selected="false" class=" soon text-indent" data-activeclass="soon_on" data-disabledclass="soon" data-omn="salesoon" id="onsale_soon_tab" role="tab" style="display:inline; " tabindex="-1">
            Próximamente
           </li>
          </ul>
          <script>
           var onsaleTabs = (function($){
                 var $currentTab = $('#js-onsale-tab').find("li").first(),
                     $tabList = $('#js-onsale-tab'),
                     $wrapper = $('#onSaleWrap');
             
                 var tabs = {
                     showTab: function($tab){                       
                         if($currentTab[0] == $tab[0]){
                             return false;
                         }
                         $currentTab.attr('aria-selected', false)
                                    .removeClass($currentTab.attr("data-activeClass"))
                                    .addClass($currentTab.attr("data-disabledClass"))
                                    .attr("tabindex", "-1");
 
                         $tab.attr('aria-selected', true)
                             .removeClass($tab.attr("data-disabledClass"))
                             .addClass($tab.attr("data-activeClass"))
                             .attr('tabindex', '0');
 
                         $("#"+ $tab.attr("aria-controls")).attr('aria-hidden', false)
                                                           .show(); 
 
                         $("#"+ $currentTab.attr("aria-controls")).hide()
                                                                  .attr('aria-hidden', true);
 
                         $currentTab = $tab;
                         $currentTab.focus();
                         omniTracking.navigation_link('tm_homeA_'+ $tab.attr("data-omn"));
                     },
                     showNext: function(){
                             this.showTab(this.getNext());
                     },
                     showPrev: function(){
                             this.showTab(this.getPrev());
                     },
                     getNext: function($tab){
                         $tab = $tab || $currentTab;
                         if( $tab.is( ":last-child" ) ){
                             return $tabList.find("li").first();
                         } else {
                             return $tab.next();
                         }
                     },
                     getPrev: function($tab){
                         $tab = $tab || $currentTab;
                         if( $tab.is( ":first-child" )){
                             return $tabList.find("li").last();
                         } else {
                             return $tab.prev();
                         }
                     },
                     getCurrentTab: function(){
                         return $currentTab;
                     },
                     attachEvents: function(){
                         var self = this;
 
                         $tabList.delegate("li", "click", function(){
                            self.showTab($(this));
                         }).delegate("li", "keydown",function(event){
                             var isCtrl = (event.ctrlKey ? true : false),
                                 prevent = false;
                             switch(event.which){
                                 case 13: case 32: // enter key | spacebar
                                     self.showTab($(this));
                                     prevent = true;
                                     break;
                                 case 37: case 38: // arrow-left | arrow-down
                                     if (isCtrl){
                                         self.getPrev($(this)).focus();
                                     } else {
                                         self.showPrev();
                                     }
                                     prevent = true;
                                     break;
                                 case 39: case 40: // arrow-right | arrow-top
                                     if (isCtrl){
                                         self.getNext($(this)).focus();
                                     } else {
                                         self.showNext();
                                     }
                                     prevent = true;
                                     break;
                             }
                             return !prevent; 
                         });
                     }
                 };
 
                 tabs.attachEvents();
                 return tabs;
             })(jQuery)
          </script>

         <script language="JavaScript">
          if(!window.member_data) {
                    var member_data = new Hash();
                 }
                 var greet,bdy_txt;
                 var callout = [];
                 function initMyTMFav() {
                    mytmModule_generic_images = {
                       '10001':'TM_GenCatImgs_Music_BW.jpg',
                       '10002':'TM_GenCatImgs_ArtsTheatre_BW.jpg',
                       '10003':'TM_GenCatImgs_Family_BW.jpg',
                       '10004':'TM_GenCatImgs_Sports_BW.jpg',
                       '10005':'TM_GenCatImgs_Generic_BW.jpg',
                       '10012':'TM_GenCatImgs_Generic_BW.jpg'
                    }
                     var mid_val = GetCookie('MID');
                     if( !mid_val || mid_val.empty() ) {
                         $('loading_lb_mytm').hide();
                         $('greeting').innerHTML = 'Hola.';
                         $('mytm_body').innerHTML = '¡Actualiza tu lista de favoritos y no te pierdas ningún evento!';
                         $('mytm_link').innerHTML = '<a href="https://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/member/addfavs?tm_link=tm_homeA_mytm_signin">Entra</a> o <a href="https://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/member/?tm_link=tm_homeA_mytm_create&identity_login_do_signup=1">Crea tu cuenta</a>';
                     }
                     else {
                         var dma_val = GetCookie('NDMA');
                         if( $('lcl_venue_callout') ) {
                             $('lcl_venue_callout').show();
                         }
                         if (!member_data.get('member')) {
                             getMember('/json/member', member_data, 'member');
                         }
                         new PeriodicalExecuter(
                             function(pe) {
                                 if( member_data.get('member') ) {
                                     pe.stop();
                                     var mem_data = member_data.get('member');
                                     var mem_faves;
                                     var mem_fave_size;
                                     var not_natl_dma = false;
                                     if( dma_val && !dma_val.empty() && dma_val != '99999' && not_natl_dma ) {
                                         mem_faves = $H(mem_data.artists_with_events).findAll( function(t){ return t.value.dmas.include(dma_val) } );
                                     }
                                     else {
                                         mem_faves = $H(mem_data.artists_with_events);
                                     }
                                     var mem_fave_size = Object.isArray( mem_faves ) ? mem_faves.length : mem_faves.keys().length;
                                     var mem_artists = mem_data.artists.concat(mem_data.teams);
                                     greet = 'Hola ' + mem_data.first_name + '.';
                                     var total_html = new Array();
                                     if( mem_fave_size ) {
                                         callout.push('<a class="bld" href="https://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/member/addfavs?tm_link=tm_homeA_mytm_favorites">¡Actualiza tu lista de favoritos!  »</a>');
                                         if( mem_fave_size == 1 ) {
                                             bdy_txt = ' 1 de tus favoritos tiene eventos';
                                         }
                                         else {
                                             bdy_txt = ' ' + mem_fave_size  + ' de tus favoritos tienen eventos.';
                                         }
                                         total_html.push('<ul class="fav-list">');
                                         var max_disp = false;
                                         var itemMax = 2;
                                         mem_faves.sortBy( function(s){ return s.value.earliest_event_date }).each( function(f,idx) {
                                             var name = mem_artists.find( function(e) {
                                                 return e.id == f.key;
                                             });
                                             if( idx > itemMax && !max_disp ) {
                                                 max_disp = true;
                                                 if( max_disp ) {
                                                    callout.push('<a href="https://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/member?tm_link=tm_homeA_mytm_favEvent_SeeMore" class="more lh18">Ver más »</a><br>');
                                                  }
                                                  total_html.push('</ul><ul class="favs" id="moreFavs" style="display: none;">');
                                             }
                                             var pic = "http://s1.ticketm.net/tm/es-mx" + (name.image ? name.image : "/tmimages/" + mytmModule_generic_images[f.value.major_id]);
                                             total_html.push('<li><a href="' + f.value.link + '?tm_link=tm_homeA_mytm_image' + (idx + 1) + '"><img src="' + pic + '" alt="More info about ' + name.name + '" class="mytm_module_image" width="80" /></a>');
                                             total_html.push('<a href="' + f.value.link + '?tm_link=tm_homeA_artist' + (idx + 1) + '">' + name.name + '</a></li>');
                                         });
                                         total_html.push('</ul>');
                                     }
                                     else {
                                         bdy_txt = ' 0 de tus favoritos tienen eventos.';                                            callout.push('<a class="more" href="https://www.ticketmaster.com.mx/member/addfavs?tm_link=tm_homeA_mytm_favorites">¡Actualiza tu lista de favoritos</a> y no te pierdas ningún evento!');                                    }
                                     $('loading_lb_mytm').hide();
                                     $('greeting').innerHTML = greet;
                                     $('mytm_body').innerHTML = bdy_txt;                              
                                     (total_html.length > 0 ) ? $('mytm_link').insert({'before': total_html.join('')}): '';
                                     $('mytm_link').innerHTML = callout.reverse().join('');
                                 }
                             }, 0.25
                         );
                     }
                 }
                 document.observe("dom:loaded",initMyTMFav);
         </script>

         <script language="JavaScript">
          var SectionRSVPModule
         var rsvp_events = [];
         tmfb.after_load( function() {
             SectionRSVPModule = new SectionRSVPModule({'style':'section','backend':'/json/rsvp','subject':'home','page_type':4});
         });
         tmfb.after_load_failed( function() {
             if( typeof( SectionRSVPModule ) === 'object' ) {
                 SectionRSVPModule.errors.facebook = true;
                 SectionRSVPModule.show_fb_error();
             }
             else {
                 SectionRSVPModule = new SectionRSVPModule({'fb_err':true,'style':'section','backend':'/json/rsvp','subject':'home','page_type':4});
             }
         });
